VOICEWOW.
 
 Sarcastic. Irreverent. Bold. And still waiting for his billion dollar bail-out.
 
 Leon Flood is an American voiceover artist who has gained worldwide acclaim for his dramatic tone, huge sound, and unique sarcasm on demand. In a world of sound-alike announcers, Leon's signature sarcasm cuts across the airwaves and internet like an incinerator devouring paper. He also cooks a mean smoked brisket. . . He's SO Emo.
 
 You've heard his work thundering across stations worldwide since 1991, including KBIG Los Angeles, KYW TV Philadelphia, Energy 108 Belfast, KZZP Phoenix, WBLI Long Island, WWWW Detroit, KOMP Las Vegas, and literally hundreds more. From movie trailers to radio and television promos, commercials to live events, Leon has done em all. Twice if it felt good. Program directors worldwide are united in their opinion: GIVE ME MORE!
 
 Extra helpings of sarcasm and attitude at no additional cost. His parents are sooo proud. . . 
 
 Leon and his family live near Tampa Florida in one of those quaint little drinking towns that is afflicted with a severe fishing problem.
 
 Add him to your station. It's what ALL the cool kids are doing these days. ?   ďVerdana    	ł  đwűŘ°PXí(ďÜ    ˙       (  Shamwow? VOICEWOW.
 
 Sarcastic. Irreverent. Bold. And still waiting for HIS billion-dollar bail-out.
 
 Leon Flood is an American voiceover artist who has gained worldwide acclaim for his dramatic tone, huge sound, and unique sarcasm on demand. In a world of sound-alike announcers, Leon's signature sarcasm cuts across the airwaves and internet like an incinerator devouring paper. He also cooks a mean smoked brisket. . . He's SO Emo.
 
 You've heard his work thundering across stations worldwide since 1991, including KBIG Los Angeles, KYW TV Philadelphia, Energy 108 Belfast, KZZP Phoenix, WBLI Long Island, WWWW Detroit, KOMP Las Vegas, and literally hundreds more. From movie trailers to radio and television promos, commercials to live events, Leon has done em all. Twice if it felt good. Program directors worldwide are united in their opinion: GIVE ME MORE!
 
 Extra helpings of sarcasm and attitude at no additional cost. His parents are sooo proud. . . 
 
 Leon and his family live near Tampa Florida in one of those quaint little drinking towns that is afflicted with a severe fishing problem.
